Some little examples from the LondonR GGVis workshop

Obviously the examples here are leagues better than this:
http://ggvis.rstudio.com/ggvis-basics.html

###The Data

{% highlight r %}
setwd("~/Documents/RStudioProjects/GGVis")
tubeData = read.csv("tubeData.csv")
head(tubeData)
{% endhighlight %}



{% highlight text %}
#>       Line Month Scheduled Excess TOTAL Opened Length Type Stations
#> 1 Bakerloo     1     29.42   6.04 35.46   1906   23.2   DT       25
#> 2 Bakerloo     2     29.42   6.54 35.96   1906   23.2   DT       25
#> 3 Bakerloo     3     29.30   4.77 34.08   1906   23.2   DT       25
#> 4 Bakerloo     4     29.30   5.40 34.70   1906   23.2   DT       25
#> 5 Bakerloo     5     29.30   5.23 34.53   1906   23.2   DT       25
#> 6 Bakerloo     6     29.30   5.03 34.33   1906   23.2   DT       25
{% endhighlight %}


###Basics

{% highlight r %}
ggvis(tubeData, ~Month, ~Excess)
{% endhighlight %}

{% highlight r %}
mtcars %>%
  ggvis(~wt, ~mpg) %>%
  layer_points(fill = ~factor(cyl), shape:= "triangle") %>%
  layer_smooths(stroke := "blue") %>%
  layer_model_predictions(model = "lm", stroke := "red")
{% endhighlight %}



{% highlight text %}

#Controlling axis and legends

{% highlight r %}
tubeData %>%
  ggvis(~Month, ~Excess) %>%
  add_axis("x", title = "Month") %>%
  layer_points(fill = ~Line)
